<section class="result-section oxford-container need-collapse" data-nav-text="牛津词典" data-collapse-height="700" data-forbin-select="y">   <header class="section-header">牛津词典</header> <div id="cont-entry" class="details-cont-item details-cont-item-tail item-oxford">   <div class="oxford-entry f-result">    <div class="entry-pg f-gap-top-large">    <div class="entry-p entry-p-ib"> <p class="f-title f-title-bold pg-p f-gap-top">verb</p>  </div>       <p class="entry-d f-gap-top">    <span class="entry-info"><span class="entry-info-left">(</span>formal<span class="entry-info-right">)</span></span>    <span class="entry-pts">[<span class="entry-hover data-hover-tip" data-hover-tip-text="动词+名词短语">VN</span>]</span>   产生；表现；显示 <br> to produce or show sth  </p>         <div class="entry-x f-color-brown f-gap-top"> <p class="entry-x-en">  He emanates power and confidence.<a href="javascript:void(0);" data-sound-lan="en" data-sound-text="He%20emanates%20power%20and%20confidence." class="operate-btn op-sound"><span class="icon-sound"></span></a> </p> <p class="entry-x-zh"> 他表现出力量和信心。 </p> </div>         <div class="entry-drg f-gap-top-large">   <span class="entry-bracket-ch">【</span>派生词】<span class="word-can-trans"><a class="f-link sec-trans" href="/#en/zh/emanation" data-stat-id="45">emanation</a></span>    <span class="dr-p f-gap-top">noun</span>     <div class="entry-alone f-gap-top">   <span class="entry-grs">[<span class="entry-hover data-hover-tip" data-hover-tip-text="可数名词">C</span>, <span class="entry-hover data-hover-tip" data-hover-tip-text="不可数名词">U</span>]</span>   </div>    </div>       <div class="entry-pvsg entry-card f-overflow-hidden f-gap-top-large"> <div class="f-card f-card-with-tag"> <span class="entry-card-tag">短语动词</span>  <div class="entry-pvg">   <p class="pvg-pv">emanate from sth</p>     <p class="entry-d f-gap-top">   发源于；从…发出 <br> to come from sth or somewhere  </p>           <div class="entry-xr f-gap-top"> 同义词： <span class="word-can-trans"><a href="/#en/zh/issue%20from" class="f-link sec-trans" data-stat-id="45">issue from</a></span> </div>        <div class="entry-x f-color-brown f-gap-top"> <p class="entry-x-en">  The sound of loud music emanated from the building.<a href="javascript:void(0);" data-sound-lan="en" data-sound-text="The%20sound%20of%20loud%20music%20emanated%20from%20the%20building." class="operate-btn op-sound"><span class="icon-sound"></span></a> </p> <p class="entry-x-zh"> 喧闹的音乐声是从那栋楼房里传出来的。 </p> </div>        <div class="entry-x f-color-brown f-gap-top"> <p class="entry-x-en">  The proposal originally emanated from the UN.<a href="javascript:void(0);" data-sound-lan="en" data-sound-text="The%20proposal%20originally%20emanated%20from%20the%20UN." class="operate-btn op-sound"><span class="icon-sound"></span></a> </p> <p class="entry-x-zh"> 这个建议最初是由联合国提出的。 </p> </div> class="result-section need-collapse" data-nav-text="柯林斯词典" data-collapse-height="700"> <header class="section-header">柯林斯词典</header> <div id="cont-collins" class="details-cont-item item-collins collins"> <div class="collins-wrap">  <ul class="collins-item">     <li class="collins-type-item item-mean"> <h4 class="mean-title">  <span class="mean-id">1</span>  <div class="mean-content">   <span class="mean-posp">V-ERG</span>   <span class="mean-tran">表现出;散发;流露</span> <br>  <span class="mean-def">If a quality <b>emanates from</b> you, or if you <b>emanate</b> a quality, you give people a strong sense that you have that quality.</span>       </div> </h4>   <div class="mean-example"> <p>Intelligence and cunning emanated from him...<a href="javascript:void(0);" class="operate-btn class="mean-content">   <span class="mean-posp">VERB</span>   <span class="mean-tran">来自(于);(从…)散发出</span> <br>  <span class="mean-def">If something <b>emanates from</b> somewhere, it comes from there.</span>       </div> </h4>   <div class="mean-example"> <p>The heady aroma of wood fires emanated from the stove.<a href="javascript:void(0);" class="operate-btn op-sound"><span class="ras-type f-gap-top">词根</span>  <div class="ras-coin"> <span class="ras-content">man(i), manu</span><span class="ras-indicate">= hand 手</span> </div>  </div>    <div class="ras-normal f-gap-top-large">   <div class="para-ras ras-mean">  <div class="ex-ras">   <div class="ex-part"> <p> <span class="ex-word">emanate</span> <span class="ex-p">v.</span> <span class="ex-d">散发；发出</span> <span class="ex-p">n.</span> <span class="ex-d">手铐；束缚</span> </p>  <p> <span class="ex-dec">man 手 + acle 表物 → 手上的东西 → 手铐</span> </p>  </div>   </div>  <div class="ex-ras f-gap-top-large">   <div class="ex-part"> <p> <span class="ex-word">manage</span> <span class="ex-p">v.</span> <span class="ex-d">处理；管理</span> </p>  <p> <span class="ex-dec">man 手 + age 表行为 → 用手做 → 处理；引申为管理</span> </p>  </div>   </div>  <div class="ex-ras f-gap-top-large">   <div class="ex-part"> <p> <span class="ex-word">maniacal</span> <span class="ex-p">adj.</span> <span class="ex-d">狂热的</span> </p>  <p> <span <div class="extra-wrap" style="top: 455px; display: block;">
<a href="feedback" class="feedback-btn extra-btn" id="index-feedback-btn">意见反馈</a>
<a href="###" class="backtotop-btn extra-btn" style="display: block;"></a>
</div>
<script type="text/javascript">
    /**
     * @function :  插件的调用。
     * @how2use  :  使用过程，可以复制过去，仅需修改调用按钮id即可；如需透传数据信息，请联系百度反馈接口人。
     */
    (function () {
        /**
         * @function :第一次加载插件，之后调用插件
         */
        function init_feedback() {
            if (bds && bds.qa && bds.qa.ShortCut && bds.qa.ShortCut.initRightBar) {
                //初始化反馈插件的样式参数

                var fb_options = {
                    needImage: true,   //是否需要用户展示图片(截图，或者上传)
                    upload_file: false,   //是否选择上传图片， true 表示上传图片，false表示截图
                    appid: 215648,   //产品线的id
                    productLine: 20060,   //
                    wenjuanTitle: "",   //问卷调查标题
                    wenjuanURL: "",   //问卷调查链接
                    issuePlaceholder: "请您描述遇到的问题或意见建议",   //问题描述提示语
                    contactPlaceholder: "请输入邮件、手机号码或QQ号码任意一种联系方式",   //联系方式提示语
                    showPosition: "bottom_right",   //显示位置，中心：center，右下： bottom_right
                    contactWayType: "contact_way",   //联系方式类型 contact_way，email，qq，tel
                    needContactWay: true,   //是否显示联系方式
                    needHotQuestion: false,   //是否显示常见问题
                    needQuestionnaire: false,   //是否显示问卷调查
                    needFeedbackType: true,   //是否显示反馈类型
                    needProductType: false,   //是否显示问题类型
                    needEvaluate: true,   //是否启用用户评价
                    typeArray: [{"id":"34174","name":"翻译质量问题"},{"id":"34175","name":"发音问题"},{"id":"34176","name":"意见建议或其它"},{"id":"34177","name":"词典问题"},{"id":"34180","name":"使用咨询"}],   //下拉列表项
                    titleBgColor: "#FFFFFF",   //标题栏背景色
                    buttonColor: "#3582FA",   //按钮的颜色
                    mainFontColor: "#151515",   //文字的主体颜色
                    secondaryFontColor: "#999999",   //文字的辅助颜色(用于input textarea输入框的提示文本)
                    titleColor: "#333333",   //标题栏颜色
                    hotQuestionArray: [],  //启用常见问题，列举常见的问题 <=5 个
                    needNoticeTips: true,  //是否显示通告文案
                    noticeTips: '百度翻译官方反馈QQ群：289656304', //通告文案
                };

                bds.qa.ShortCut.initRightBar(fb_options);
                //产品线需要透传的参数，注意：json的标题必须是规范json写法，双引号，最后无逗号
                var pro_data = {
                    //"extend_feedback_channel": 0  // 反馈来源
                };
                bds.qa.ShortCut._getProData(pro_data);
            }
        }

        /**
         * @function :校验js加载完成
         * @returns :{boolean}
         */
        function loadRightBar() {
            _hmt.push(['_trackEvent', '首页', 'web端意见反馈按钮点击']);
            if (window.bds&&window.bds.qa&&window.bds.qa.ShortCut) {
                init_feedback();
            } else {
                loadScript(
                    "https://ufosdk.baidu.com/Public/feedback/js/dist/feedback_plugin_2.0.js",
                    function () {
                        init_feedback();
                    }, {
                        charset: "utf-8",
                        id: "feedback_script"
                    });
            }
            return false;
        }
        document
            .getElementById("index-feedback-btn")
            .onclick = loadRightBar;
    })();
    // 页面加载脚本判定函数
    function loadScript(url, callback, opt) {
        var script = document.createElement("script");
        var opt = opt || {};
        script.type = "text/javascript";
        if (opt.charset) {
            script.charset = opt.charset;
        }
        if (opt.id) {
            script.id = opt.id;
        }

        if (script.readyState) {
            script.onreadystatechange = function () {
                if (script.readyState == "loaded" || script.readyState == "complete") {
                    script.onreadystatechange = null;
                    callback();
                }
            };
        } else {
            script.onload = function () {
                callback();
            };
        }
        script.src = url;
        document.body.appendChild(script);
    }
</script>
